* **AI**: ## Implementation Summary
  
  Implemented the Week 1 design specifications from the `52vibes` project:
  
  ### 1. crush-export (Go CLI Tool)
  - **Location**: `crush-export/`
  - **Features**:
    - Uses `modernc.org/sqlite` (CGO-free)
    - Repository pattern for database access
    - Markdown export with statistics, key exchanges, lessons learned placeholder
    - CLI flags: `-db`, `-out`, `-session`, `-l`, `-version`
    - Static binary with embedded version info
  - **Tests**: All passing (db, export, model packages)
  
  ### 2. Wiki Sync (GitHub Actions)
  - **Location**: `.github/workflows/wiki-sync.yml`
  - **Features**:
    - Triggers on push to `main` affecting `sessions/`
    - Copies markdown to wiki repository
    - Conditional commit/push (only when changes exist)
    - Token security via `WIKI_TOKEN` secret
  
  ### 3. Blog Platform (Hugo)
  - **Location**: `wk1-blog/`
  - **Features**:
    - Custom `52vibes` theme with Gruvbox colors
    - tmux-inspired layout (status bar, content area, bottom nav)
    - Dark/light theme toggle (~200 bytes inline JS)
    - Community page with GitHub API (~400 bytes inline JS)
    - Security headers via `_headers` file
    - Responsive breakpoints (mobile/tablet/desktop)
    - Accessibility: skip links, ARIA landmarks, focus indicators
    - SEO: meta tags, JSON-LD, RSS, sitemap
  
  ### 4. Community Features
  - **Location**: `wk1-blog/content/community/_index.md`
  - **Features**:
    - sessionStorage caching (1 hour TTL)
    - XSS protection via text content escaping
    - Graceful degradation (noscript fallback)
    - Rate limit error handling

--bg-soft: #f2e5bc;\n  --fg: #3c3836;\n  --fg-soft: #504945;\n  --accent: #d65d0e;\n  --accent-alt: #af3a03;\n  --border: #d5c4a1;\n}\n\`\`\`\n\n### Layout Structure\n\`\`\`html\n\u003cbody\u003e\n  \u003cheader class=\"status-bar\"\u003e\u003c!-- Week indicator, section --\u003e\u003c/header\u003e\n  \u003cmain class=\"content-area\"\u003e\u003c!-- Bordered content --\u003e\u003c/main\u003e\n  \u003cnav class=\"bottom-nav\"\u003e\u003c!-- Navigation links --\u003e\u003c/nav\u003e\n\u003c/body\u003e\n\`\`\`\n\n### Constraints\n* Theme MUST be standalone with no parent dependencies\n* Main content MUST have visible CSS border\n* All colors MUST use CSS custom properties\n\n---\n\n## Design: Asset Pipeline #BLOG_ASSETS_0001 #BLOG_ASSETS_0002 #BLOG_ASSETS_0003\n\n### Overview\nZero-dependency asset processing using Hugo Pipes for CSS, self-hosted fonts, and minimal inline JavaScript.\n\n### Components\n* **assets/css/** - SCSS/CSS source files\n* **static/fonts/** - IBM Plex Sans, JetBrains Mono (WOFF2)\n* **Inline Scripts** - Theme toggle (1KB)\n\n### Font Loading\n\`\`\`css\n@font-face {\n  font-family: 'IBM Plex Sans';\n  src: url('/fonts/IBMPlexSans-Regular.woff2') format('woff2');\n  font-weight: 400;\n  font-display: swap;\n}\n\`\`\`\n\n### Constraints\n* CSS MUST be processed via Hugo Pipes only\n* Font files MUST be self-hosted\n* All \`@font-face\` MUST include \`font-display: swap\`\n* Total inline JavaScript MUST NOT exceed 1024 bytes\n* Core functionality MUST work without JavaScript\n\n---\n\n## Design: Responsive Layout System #BLOG_RESP_0001 #BLOG_RESP_0002\n\n### Overview\nMobile-first responsive design with defined breakpoints and touch-friendly targets.\n\n### Breakpoints\n* Mobile: 0-767px\n* Tablet: 768-1023px\n* Desktop: 1024px+\n\n### Constraints\n* Media queries MUST use \`min-width\` (mobile-first)\n* All interactive elements MUST have minimum 44x44px touch target\n* Status bar week numbers MUST be touch-friendly on mobile\n\n---\n\n## Design: Accessibility Implementation #BLOG_A11Y_0001 #BLOG_A11Y_0002 #BLOG_A11Y_0003 #BLOG_A11Y_0004\n\n### Overview\nWCAG-compliant accessibility features including semantic HTML, skip links, focus management.\n\n### Structure\n\`\`\`html\n\u003cbody\u003e\n  \u003ca href=\"#main-content\" class=\"skip-link\"\u003eSkip to main content\u003c/a\u003e\n  \u003cheader role=\"banner\"\u003e...\u003c/header\u003e\n  \u003cnav aria-label=\"Main navigation\"\u003e...\u003c/nav\u003e\n  \u003cmain id=\"main-content\"\u003e\n    \u003carticle\u003e\n      \u003ch1\u003ePost Title\u003c/h1\u003e\n      \u003caside aria-label=\"Table of contents\"\u003e...\u003c/aside\u003e\n    \u003c/article\u003e\n  \u003c/main\u003e\n  \u003cfooter\u003e\n    \u003cnav aria-label=\"Footer navigation\"\u003e...\u003c/nav\u003e\n  \u003c/footer\u003e\n\u003c/body\u003e\n\`\`\`\n\n### Constraints\n* Heading hierarchy MUST be sequential (h1h2h3)\n* Skip link MUST be first focusable element\n* Focus indicators MUST be visible (minimum 2px)\n* Multiple \`\u003cnav\u003e\` elements MUST have unique \`aria-label\`\n\n---\n\n## Design: Security Headers #BLOG_SEC_0001 #BLOG_SEC_0002 #BLOG_SEC_0003\n\n### Overview\nSecurity configuration via Cloudflare Pages \`_headers\` file.\n\n### Headers File\n\`\`\`\n/*\n  Content-Security-Policy: default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; img-src 'self' data: https:; font-src 'self'; connect-src 'self' https://api.github.com\n  Strict-Transport-Security: max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains\n  X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff\n  X-Frame-Options: DENY\n  Referrer-Policy: strict-origin-when-cross-origin\n  Permissions-Policy: geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()\n\`\`\`\n\n---\n\n## Design: Navigation Components #BLOG_NAV_0001 #BLOG_NAV_0002 #BLOG_NAV_0003 #BLOG_NAV_0004\n\n### Overview\nNavigation system including status bar, bottom navigation, TOC, and post pagination.\n\n### Status Bar\n* Week numbers as \`\u003ca\u003e\` (completed) or \`\u003cspan\u003e\` (upcoming)\n* Each completed week link has \`title\` attribute\n\n### Bottom Navigation\n* Required links: About, Weeks, Reports, RSS, GitHub\n* \`aria-label=\"Footer navigation\"\`\n\n### Post Navigation\n* Previous/Next using Hugo's \`.PrevInSection\`, \`.NextInSection\`\n* Week 1: no Previous; Latest: no Next\n\n---\n\n## Design: Content Features #BLOG_CONTENT_0001 #BLOG_CONTENT_0002 #BLOG_CONTENT_0003\n\n### Overview\nBlog post structure including front matter, syntax highlighting, and callout shortcode.\n\n### Required Front Matter\n\`\`\`yaml\n---\ntitle: \"Week 1: Building Infrastructure\"\ndate: 2026-01-05T10:00:00-08:00\nweek: 1\nquarter: 1\ntheme: \"Agentic Infrastructure\"\ndescription: \"...\"\nsession_log: \"https://github.com/owner/52vibes/wiki/...\"\nrepository: \"https://github.com/owner/52vibes\"\n---\n\`\`\`\n\n### Callout Shortcode\n\`\`\`markdown\n{{\u003c callout type=\"tip\" \u003e}}\nThis is a helpful tip.\n{{\u003c /callout \u003e}}\n\`\`\`\n\n---\n\n## Design: SEO and Discovery #BLOG_SEO_0001 #BLOG_SEO_0002 #BLOG_SEO_0003 #BLOG_SEO_0004\n\n### Overview\nSEO through meta tags, JSON-LD structured data, RSS feeds, and sitemap.\n\n### Meta Tags\n* Title, description, OG, and Twitter meta tags on all pages\n* JSON-LD BlogPosting schema for posts\n* RSS at \`/blog/index.xml\`\n* Sitemap at \`/sitemap.xml\`\n\n---\n\n## Design: Theme Toggle #BLOG_TOGGLE_0001\n\n### Overview\nDark/light theme switching with localStorage persistence.\n\n### Implementation\n\`\`\`javascript\n(function(){\n  const key = '52vibes-theme';\n  const html = document.documentElement;\n  const saved = localStorage.getItem(key);\n  const sys = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)').matches ? 'light' : 'dark';\n  html.dataset.theme = saved || sys;\n  \n  document.getElementById('theme-toggle').onclick = function() {\n    const next = html.dataset.theme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark';\n    html.dataset.theme = next;\n    localStorage.setItem(key, next);\n  };\n})();\n\`\`\`\n\n---\n\n---\n\n# Implementation TODOs\n\nDONE: Initialize Hugo Project Structure #BLOG001
